========================================================================

── STRUCTURE ──

  Phase:            polycrystalline, grain boundaries present

── COMPOSITION ──
  Gd₅(SiₓGe₁₋ₓ)₄ (giant magnetocaloric)
  Components:       multi-component (HEA / perovskite)

── PROCESSING ──
1. Precursor: Gd₅(SiₓGe₁₋ₓ)₄ (giant magnetocaloric)
2. Primary: quench / rapid solidification (one-pot / in-situ)
3. Interface engineering: dynamic bonding cycle (heat-cool 3×)

── INTERFACES ──
  Coupling:         moderate (H-bond, π-π) (50-150 kJ/mol)
  Reversible:       partially

── PROPERTIES ──
  Young modulus GPa              1-50 (flexible)
  Tensile strength MPa           10-300
  Thermal conductivity WmK       1-50
  Electrical resistivity         nonlinear, χ-divergent near Tc
  Self healing efficiency        none

── TOPOLOGICAL PROTECTION ──
  Invariant:        trivial
  Protection:       none
  Edge states:      none
  Robustness:       fragile

── CRITICALITY ──
  Regime:           critical (self-modeling)
  Response:         χ ~ |T-Tc|^(-γ)
  Application:      sensor / actuator

── MEMORY ──
  Type:             none (Markov-0)
  Hysteresis:       False
  History:          no path dependence

── TARGET APPLICATIONS ──
  1. Ultra-sensitive strain sensor (self-referencing)
  2. Critical-point actuator (χ-divergent response)
  3. Self-healing structural composite

  IG Type: ⟨𐑼𐑥𐑾𐑬𐑐𐑧𐑲𐑠𐑮𐑫𐑳𐑭⟩
  Ouroboricity: O₂  |  Frobenius Score: 0.65
========================================================================

── STRUCTURE ──
  Dimensionality:   bulk solid / composite (macro)
  Topology:         bowtie/crossing — interpenetrating / woven
  Symmetry:         partially ordered (Z₂)
  Phase:            single crystal, ultrahigh vacuum processed

── COMPOSITION ──
  (Bi,Sb)₂(Te,Se)₃ ternary topological insulator
  Components:       multi-component (HEA / perovskite)

── PROCESSING ──
1. Precursor: (Bi,Sb)₂(Te,Se)₃ ternary topological insulator
2. Primary: slow anneal / float zone (sequential / layer-by-layer)
3. Interface engineering: dynamic bonding cycle (heat-cool 3×)
4. Topology: ultrahigh vacuum (10⁻¹⁰ torr), epitaxial growth
5. Memory training: full path encoding cycling protocol

── INTERFACES ──
  Coupling:         dynamic (Diels-Alder, disulfide) (100-300 kJ/mol)
  Reversible:       True

── PROPERTIES ──
  Young modulus GPa              50-200 (moderate)
  Tensile strength MPa           300-1000
  Thermal conductivity WmK       10-100 (phonon-dominated, edge-channel)
  Electrical resistivity         surface: metallic (~h/e²), bulk: insulating
  Self healing efficiency        85-95% (thermal trigger)
  Healing cycles                 50-200
  Shape memory strain pct        6-10% (full recovery)
  Transformation temperature C   -50 to +200
  Topological invariant          topological (Chern)
  Edge state type                chiral, quantized
  Robustness                     disorder-immune

── TOPOLOGICAL PROTECTION ──
  Invariant:        ℤ (integer winding)
  Protection:       topological (Chern)
  Edge states:      chiral, quantized
  Robustness:       disorder-immune

── CRITICALITY ──
  Regime:           complex-plane critical
  Response:         damped oscillations
  Application:      tunable filter / resonator

── MEMORY ──
  Type:             eternal / shape-memory
  Hysteresis:       persistent
  History:          full path encoding

── TARGET APPLICATIONS ──
  1. Topological quantum computing substrate
  2. Dissipationless interconnects (edge channels)
  3. Self-healing structural composite
  4. Shape-memory actuator / deployable structure
  5. Morphing aerospace structure (full path memory)
  6. Quantum sensing / qubit host

── COMPOSITION ──
  (Bi,Sb)₂(Te,Se)₃ ternary topological insulator
  Components:       multi-component (HEA / perovskite)

── PROCESSING ──
1. Precursor: (Bi,Sb)₂(Te,Se)₃ ternary topological insulator
2. Primary: slow anneal / float zone (one-pot / in-situ)
3. Interface engineering: dynamic bonding cycle (heat-cool 3×)
4. Topology: ultrahigh vacuum (10⁻¹⁰ torr), epitaxial growth
5. Memory training: two prior states cycling protocol

── INTERFACES ──
  Coupling:         weak (van der Waals) (< 50 kJ/mol)
  Reversible:       True

── PROPERTIES ──
  Young modulus GPa              1-50 (flexible)
  Tensile strength MPa           10-300
  Thermal conductivity WmK       10-100 (phonon-dominated, edge-channel)
  Electrical resistivity         surface: metallic (~h/e²), bulk: insulating
  Self healing efficiency        none
  Shape memory strain pct        4-8%
  Topological invariant          topological (Chern)
  Edge state type                chiral, quantized
  Robustness                     disorder-immune

── TOPOLOGICAL PROTECTION ──
  Invariant:        ℤ (integer winding)
  Protection:       topological (Chern)
  Edge states:      chiral, quantized
  Robustness:       disorder-immune

── CRITICALITY ──
  Regime:           complex-plane critical
  Response:         damped oscillations
  Application:      tunable filter / resonator

── MEMORY ──
  Type:             two-step
  Hysteresis:       double loop / training effect
  History:          two prior states

── TARGET APPLICATIONS ──
  1. Topological quantum computing substrate
  2. Dissipationless interconnects (edge channels)
  3. Self-healing structural composite
  4. Shape-memory actuator / deployable structure

  IG Type: ⟨𐑦𐑶𐑩𐑹𐑱𐑧𐑔𐑠𐑮𐑫𐑙𐑭⟩
  Ouroboricity: O₂  |  Frobenius Score: 0.70
========================================================================

── STRUCTURE ──
  Dimensionality:   self-similar metamaterial (nm to cm)
  Topology:         interpenetrating — IPN / MOF@COF
  Symmetry:         Frobenius-closed
  Phase:            polycrystalline, grain boundaries present

── COMPOSITION ──
  Bi₂Se₃ or Sb₂Te₃ (3D topological insulator)
  Components:       unary (pure element / compound)

── PROCESSING ──
1. Precursor: Bi₂Se₃ or Sb₂Te₃ (3D topological insulator)
2. Primary: slow anneal / float zone (sequential / layer-by-layer)
3. Interface engineering: dynamic bonding cycle (heat-cool 3×)
4. Topology: ultrahigh vacuum (10⁻¹⁰ torr), epitaxial growth
5. Memory training: full path encoding cycling protocol

── INTERFACES ──
  Coupling:         weak (van der Waals) (< 50 kJ/mol)
  Reversible:       True

── PROPERTIES ──
  Young modulus GPa              1-50 (flexible)
  Tensile strength MPa           10-300
  Thermal conductivity WmK       10-100 (phonon-dominated, edge-channel)
  Electrical resistivity         surface: metallic (~h/e²), bulk: insulating
  Self healing efficiency        > 99% (autonomous, μ∘δ=id)
  Healing cycles                 unlimited (Frobenius-closed)
  Shape memory strain pct        6-10% (full recovery)
  Transformation temperature C   -50 to +200
  Topological invariant          topological (Chern)
  Edge state type                chiral, quantized
  Robustness                     disorder-immune

── TOPOLOGICAL PROTECTION ──
  Invariant:        ℤ (integer winding)
  Protection:       topological (Chern)
  Edge states:      chiral, quantized
  Robustness:       disorder-immune

── CRITICALITY ──
  Regime:           complex-plane critical
  Response:         damped oscillations
  Application:      tunable filter / resonator

── MEMORY ──
  Type:             eternal / shape-memory
  Hysteresis:       persistent
  History:          full path encoding

── TARGET APPLICATIONS ──
  1. Topological quantum computing substrate
  2. Dissipationless interconnects (edge channels)
  3. Self-healing structural composite
  4. Autonomous damage-repair coating
  5. Self-verifying critical infrastructure material
  6. Shape-memory actuator / deployable structure
  7. Morphing aerospace structure (full path memory)
  8. Hierarchical impact absorber (nano to macro)

── STRUCTURE ──
  Dimensionality:   bulk solid / composite (macro)
  Topology:         bowtie/crossing — interpenetrating / woven
  Symmetry:         partially ordered (Z₂)
  Phase:            polycrystalline, grain boundaries present

── COMPOSITION ──
  (Bi,Sb)₂(Te,Se)₃ ternary topological insulator
  Components:       multi-component (HEA / perovskite)

── PROCESSING ──
1. Precursor: (Bi,Sb)₂(Te,Se)₃ ternary topological insulator
2. Primary: slow anneal / float zone (combinatorial)
3. Interface engineering: controlled atmosphere bonding
4. Topology: ultrahigh vacuum (10⁻¹⁰ torr), epitaxial growth
5. Memory training: full path encoding cycling protocol

── INTERFACES ──
  Coupling:         strong (covalent, ionic) (150-800 kJ/mol)
  Reversible:       False

── PROPERTIES ──
  Young modulus GPa              200-400 (stiff)
  Tensile strength MPa           1000-3000
  Thermal conductivity WmK       10-100 (phonon-dominated, edge-channel)
  Electrical resistivity         surface: metallic (~h/e²), bulk: insulating
  Self healing efficiency        none
  Shape memory strain pct        6-10% (full recovery)
  Transformation temperature C   -50 to +200
  Topological invariant          topological (Chern)
  Edge state type                chiral, quantized
  Robustness                     disorder-immune

── TOPOLOGICAL PROTECTION ──
  Invariant:        ℤ (integer winding)
  Protection:       topological (Chern)
  Edge states:      chiral, quantized
  Robustness:       disorder-immune

── CRITICALITY ──
  Regime:           complex-plane critical
  Response:         damped oscillations
  Application:      tunable filter / resonator

── MEMORY ──
  Type:             eternal / shape-memory
  Hysteresis:       persistent
  History:          full path encoding

── TARGET APPLICATIONS ──
  1. Topological quantum computing substrate
  2. Dissipationless interconnects (edge channels)
  3. Shape-memory actuator / deployable structure
  4. Morphing aerospace structure (full path memory)

  Dimensionality:   bulk solid / composite (macro)
  Topology:         core-shell — coated / encapsulated
  Symmetry:         fully symmetric
  Phase:            polycrystalline, grain boundaries present

── COMPOSITION ──
  Epoxy-amine with Diels-Alder adducts (self-healing)
  Components:       binary (alloy / compound pair)

── PROCESSING ──

2. Primary: slow anneal / float zone (sequential / layer-by-layer)
3. Interface engineering: dynamic bonding cycle (heat-cool 3×)
4. Topology: ultrahigh vacuum (10⁻¹⁰ torr), epitaxial growth
5. Memory training: most recent state only cycling protocol

── INTERFACES ──
  Coupling:         dynamic (Diels-Alder, disulfide) (100-300 kJ/mol)
  Reversible:       True

── PROPERTIES ──
  Young modulus GPa              50-200 (moderate)
  Tensile strength MPa           300-1000
  Thermal conductivity WmK       10-100 (phonon-dominated, edge-channel)
  Electrical resistivity         edge: ~h/2e² quantized
  Self healing efficiency        85-95% (thermal trigger)
  Healing cycles                 50-200
  Shape memory strain pct        4-8%
  Topological invariant          symmetry-protected
  Edge state type                helical / Dirac
  Robustness                     defect-tolerant

── TOPOLOGICAL PROTECTION ──
  Invariant:        Z₂ (parity)
  Protection:       symmetry-protected
  Edge states:      helical / Dirac
  Robustness:       defect-tolerant

── CRITICALITY ──
  Regime:           complex-plane critical
  Response:         damped oscillations
  Application:      tunable filter / resonator

── MEMORY ──
  Type:             one-step
  Hysteresis:       simple loop
  History:          most recent state only

── TARGET APPLICATIONS ──
  1. Topological quantum computing substrate
  2. Dissipationless interconnects (edge channels)
  3. Self-healing structural composite
  4. Shape-memory actuator / deployable structure

  IG Type: ⟨𐑨𐑡𐑩𐑬𐑱𐑧𐑚𐑠𐑮𐑫𐑳𐑭⟩
  Ouroboricity: O₂  |  Frobenius Score: 0.35
========================================================================

── STRUCTURE ──
  Dimensionality:   thin film / membrane (monolayer to μm)
  Topology:         network — percolating network / aerogel
  Symmetry:         partially ordered (Z₂)
  Phase:            polycrystalline, grain boundaries present

── COMPOSITION ──
  (Bi,Sb)₂(Te,Se)₃ ternary topological insulator
  Components:       multi-component (HEA / perovskite)

── PROCESSING ──
1. Precursor: (Bi,Sb)₂(Te,Se)₃ ternary topological insulator
2. Primary: slow anneal / float zone (sequential / layer-by-layer)
3. Interface engineering: dynamic bonding cycle (heat-cool 3×)
4. Topology: ultrahigh vacuum (10⁻¹⁰ torr), epitaxial growth
5. Memory training: full path encoding cycling protocol

── INTERFACES ──
  Coupling:         weak (van der Waals) (< 50 kJ/mol)
  Reversible:       True

── PROPERTIES ──
  Young modulus GPa              1-50 (flexible)
  Tensile strength MPa           10-300
  Thermal conductivity WmK       10-100 (phonon-dominated, edge-channel)
  Electrical resistivity         surface: metallic (~h/e²), bulk: insulating
  Self healing efficiency        none
  Shape memory strain pct        6-10% (full recovery)
  Transformation temperature C   -50 to +200
  Topological invariant          topological (Chern)
  Edge state type                chiral, quantized
  Robustness                     disorder-immune

── TOPOLOGICAL PROTECTION ──
  Invariant:        ℤ (integer winding)
  Protection:       topological (Chern)
  Edge states:      chiral, quantized
  Robustness:       disorder-immune

── CRITICALITY ──
  Regime:           complex-plane critical
  Response:         damped oscillations
  Application:      tunable filter / resonator

── MEMORY ──
  Type:             eternal / shape-memory
  Hysteresis:       persistent
  History:          full path encoding

── TARGET APPLICATIONS ──
  1. Topological quantum computing substrate
  2. Dissipationless interconnects (edge channels)
  3. Self-healing structural composite
  4. Shape-memory actuator / deployable structure
  5. Morphing aerospace structure (full path memory)

  Ouroboricity: O₂  |  Frobenius Score: 0.90
========================================================================

── STRUCTURE ──
  Dimensionality:   thin film / membrane (monolayer to μm)
  Topology:         bowtie/crossing — interpenetrating / woven
  Symmetry:         Frobenius-closed
  Phase:            polycrystalline, grain boundaries present

── COMPOSITION ──
  CrMnFeCoNi (Cantor HEA) + self-healing microcapsules
  Components:       multi-component (HEA / perovskite)

── PROCESSING ──
1. Precursor: CrMnFeCoNi (Cantor HEA) + self-healing microcapsules
2. Primary: slow anneal / float zone (sequential / layer-by-layer)
3. Interface engineering: dynamic bonding cycle (heat-cool 3×)
4. Topology: ultrahigh vacuum (10⁻¹⁰ torr), epitaxial growth
5. Memory training: full path encoding cycling protocol

── INTERFACES ──
  Coupling:         dynamic (Diels-Alder, disulfide) (100-300 kJ/mol)
  Reversible:       True

── PROPERTIES ──
  Young modulus GPa              50-200 (moderate)
  Tensile strength MPa           300-1000
  Thermal conductivity WmK       10-100 (phonon-dominated, edge-channel)
  Electrical resistivity         surface: metallic (~h/e²), bulk: insulating
  Self healing efficiency        85-95% (thermal trigger)
  Healing cycles                 50-200
  Shape memory strain pct        6-10% (full recovery)
  Transformation temperature C   -50 to +200
  Topological invariant          topological (Chern)
  Edge state type                chiral, quantized
  Robustness                     disorder-immune

── TOPOLOGICAL PROTECTION ──
  Invariant:        ℤ (integer winding)
  Protection:       topological (Chern)
  Edge states:      chiral, quantized
  Robustness:       disorder-immune

── CRITICALITY ──
  Regime:           complex-plane critical
  Response:         damped oscillations
  Application:      tunable filter / resonator

── MEMORY ──
  Type:             eternal / shape-memory
  Hysteresis:       persistent
  History:          full path encoding

── TARGET APPLICATIONS ──
  1. Topological quantum computing substrate
  2. Dissipationless interconnects (edge channels)
  3. Self-healing structural composite
  4. Autonomous damage-repair coating
  5. Self-verifying critical infrastructure material
  6. Shape-memory actuator / deployable structure
  7. Morphing aerospace structure (full path memory)

  MATERIAL DESIGN: apache_sunrise_ceremony
  IG Type: ⟨𐑨𐑥𐑾𐑹𐑱𐑧𐑚𐑠𐑮𐑫𐑙𐑭⟩
  Ouroboricity: O₂  |  Frobenius Score: 0.90
========================================================================

── STRUCTURE ──
  Dimensionality:   thin film / membrane (monolayer to μm)
  Topology:         bowtie/crossing — interpenetrating / woven
  Symmetry:         Frobenius-closed
  Phase:            polycrystalline, grain boundaries present

── COMPOSITION ──
  Bi₂Se₃ or Sb₂Te₃ (3D topological insulator)
  Components:       unary (pure element / compound)

── PROCESSING ──
1. Precursor: Bi₂Se₃ or Sb₂Te₃ (3D topological insulator)
2. Primary: slow anneal / float zone (sequential / layer-by-layer)
3. Interface engineering: dynamic bonding cycle (heat-cool 3×)
4. Topology: ultrahigh vacuum (10⁻¹⁰ torr), epitaxial growth
5. Memory training: full path encoding cycling protocol

── INTERFACES ──
  Coupling:         dynamic (Diels-Alder, disulfide) (100-300 kJ/mol)
  Reversible:       True

── PROPERTIES ──
  Young modulus GPa              50-200 (moderate)
  Tensile strength MPa           300-1000
  Thermal conductivity WmK       10-100 (phonon-dominated, edge-channel)
  Electrical resistivity         surface: metallic (~h/e²), bulk: insulating
  Self healing efficiency        85-95% (thermal trigger)
  Healing cycles                 50-200
  Shape memory strain pct        6-10% (full recovery)
  Transformation temperature C   -50 to +200
  Topological invariant          topological (Chern)
  Edge state type                chiral, quantized
  Robustness                     disorder-immune

── TOPOLOGICAL PROTECTION ──
  Invariant:        ℤ (integer winding)
  Protection:       topological (Chern)
  Edge states:      chiral, quantized
  Robustness:       disorder-immune

── CRITICALITY ──
  Regime:           complex-plane critical
  Response:         damped oscillations
  Application:      tunable filter / resonator

── MEMORY ──
  Type:             eternal / shape-memory
  Hysteresis:       persistent
  History:          full path encoding

── TARGET APPLICATIONS ──
  1. Topological quantum computing substrate
  2. Dissipationless interconnects (edge channels)
  3. Self-healing structural composite
  4. Autonomous damage-repair coating
  5. Self-verifying critical infrastructure material
  6. Shape-memory actuator / deployable structure
  7. Morphing aerospace structure (full path memory)

  Components:       multi-component (HEA / perovskite)

── PROCESSING ──
1. Precursor: AlCoCrFeNi₂.₁ (eutectic high-entropy alloy)
2. Primary: controlled cooling (one-pot / in-situ)
3. Interface engineering: dynamic bonding cycle (heat-cool 3×)
5. Memory training: most recent state only cycling protocol

── INTERFACES ──
  Coupling:         weak (van der Waals) (< 50 kJ/mol)
  Reversible:       True

── PROPERTIES ──
  Young modulus GPa              1-50 (flexible)
  Tensile strength MPa           10-300
  Thermal conductivity WmK       1-50
  Electrical resistivity         ohmic, ρ ~ 10⁻⁶ to 10⁻² Ω·m
  Self healing efficiency        none
  Shape memory strain pct        4-8%

── TOPOLOGICAL PROTECTION ──
  Invariant:        trivial
  Protection:       none
  Edge states:      none
  Robustness:       fragile

── CRITICALITY ──
  Regime:           sub-critical / inert
  Response:         linear, no divergence
  Application:      structural material

  Hysteresis:       simple loop
  History:          most recent state only

  Type:             two-step
  Hysteresis:       double loop / training effect
  History:          two prior states

── TARGET APPLICATIONS ──
  1. Topological quantum computing substrate
  2. Dissipationless interconnects (edge channels)
  3. Shape-memory actuator / deployable structure
  4. Quantum sensing / qubit host
